# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="c7958-102">.NET Framework'teki eski türler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="c7958-103">Bu makaledeki tablolar'te eski türler listesinde [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] ve [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], derleme tarafından düzenlenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c7958-104">Eski türler ve her derlemesindeki önerilen Alternatiflerle listesini görmek için aşağıdaki bağlantıları kullanın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c7958-105">Bu tür geçersiz olduğundan, tüm üyeleri aynı zamanda artık kullanılmıyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c7958-106">.NET Framework Sınıf Kitaplığı'nda ek eski üyeler listesi için bkz: [eski üyeler](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="c7958-134">Aşağıdaki tablolarda sistem derlemelerde artık kullanılmayan bildirilen türleri listelenmektedir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c7958-135">Bu derlemeler için genel kullanılan\-amaçla .NET Framework hedefleyen uygulama geliştirme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c7958-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
